6a1(1): bsags shing / tshugs rdzogs par byas pa'i rgyu ngan/ s+thA dang / g.yodang / rdzun dang / bram dang / dag cu dang / gsod pa dang / gan pa

6a4(1): 'khor gyis bskor ba rnams dang / gnod sbyin gyi sde dper chen po lngas rtsen rang gi bu'i 'khor dang bcas pa dang / gte sprin chen po logar rdo rje rang bzhin gyi 'khor dang bcas pa dang /

6a7(1): bdag dang / klu'i rgyal por 'dres pa dang / klu'i rgyal po rgya mtsho/ rang rang gi klu'i 'khor dang bcas pang dgi dang / nam mkha' lding gi dbang po gzi chen dang / nam mkha' lding gi

282'a7(1): ngan padas rlo gyis pa dang med pa des sa rgyam bu gyis mas mas pa'i 'arnal padas bcom ldam sas kyi tha pa mang jigs pa mangs rgyam ma badzin pa mim pa ste/ las pa ma
282'b1(1): de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' gang dag la mas pas/ yan tan gyis kyang bar 'di dag dang / gzha dpag tu med pangs kyang thab pa yi dang / 'jam dpal rigs kyi bu'as rigs kyi bumo gang sa la nanas
282'b2(1): 'jig rted gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul snyed kyi dgra bcom pa mngon par shes pa drug dang ldan pa/ rnam par mthong ba brgyad la bsam gtan pa rnams la nyin cig bzhin du lha'i bas ro brgyad dang ldan pa dang / lha'i gos dag
282'b3(1): byin te/ de ltar byin pa bskal pa gang+ga'i klung gi bye ma ngag du byin pa pas/ 'jam dpal rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gzhan gang gis rang sangs rgyas gcig zas byin nang ni de bas bsod nams ches grangs med pa
282'b4(1): bskyed do// lajam dpal rigs kyi bu'am/ rigs kyi bu mo la la zhig gis sa 'jig rten gyi khams re rer gtsug lag khang 'dzam bu'i chu bo'i gser las byas pa/ nor bu ring po che glog gi phreng ba'i smras pa/ nor bu ring
282'b5(1): poche 'od thams cad bsdus pas stegs bus yongs su bskor ba/ nor bu dang / mu tig dang / rin po che'i phreng ba'i mdzes par byas sa pa/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dang sgreng ba dang / dril bu g.yer ka'i
282'b6(1): bla res bres pa/ tsAn sbrul gyi snying po'i byug pas byugs pa/ nor bu rin po che dbang gi rgyal pos khyebs par byas pa/ rgya mtsho na gnas pas rin po che rnam par dag pa/ bgod pa kun nas 'od gzer snang ba'i nor
282'b7(1): bu rin po che'i ka ba mo grogs pa/ nor bu rin po seng gi ra la ba zhes bya ba'i spang le ba bris pa/ nong bu rin po che seng ge rgyal mtshar gyis rtse mo las byas pa'i sgo gang dang rta babs dang skar khung gi brgya ba/ nga gyi
283a1(1): s+ya s+ya/ lnga lding mang po bris pa/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul snyed dag byas te/ rang sangs rgyas gnas stong phrag grangs med pa dag dang / rang sangs rgyas de dag la nyin gcig bzhin du lha'i
283a2(1): zas ro brgya dang ldan pa dang / lha'i gos dag kyang byi dang de ltar byid pa bskal pa byin pa gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed dag tu byin pa bas/ 'jam dpal rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo gzhan gang gis sangs rgyas zhe 'am/ 'jig
283a3(1): rten gyi mgon po zhe 'am/ de bzhin gshegs pa zhe 'am/ thams cad mkhyen pa zhes bya ba'i sgra thos nas/ 'di ni de bas ches bsod nams grangs med par bskyed na/ gang gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i skur mor bris pa 'am/ 
283a4(1): gzugs su byas pa mthong ba lta ci smos te/ 'di nyid ni debs ches bsod dmas grangs med par bskyed do// gang gis mar me phul ba 'am/ bdug pa 'am/ spos sam me tog gam/ rol mo'i sgra 'am/ mchod pa sna tshogs
283a5(1): gzhan dag byed pa lta ci'i spos te/ 'di nyid de bas chos bsod nams grangs med par bsgred ngo // gang gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyir nyi ma gcig bslab pa gcig bsrung ba lta ci smos te/ 'di ni de bas ches bsod nams
283a6(1): rnams grangs med par bskyed do// 'jam dpal rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo la la zhig gis de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub sems dpa' dang bcas pa/ nyan thos dang bcas pa/ phyogs bcu 'jig rten
283a7(1): kyi sa mas cad kyi thang pa rjid las pa tshig pa'i du ba'i bas brgya ldan pa/ gadzin pa 'ang cang 'phrul la/ ris pa yul la bzhal pa da'i byung gi khyis mang du 'dzu napa sas
